       </div>\n    </div>\n            </div>\n    </div>\n</div>\n<div class="lister-item mode-detail imdb-user-review  with-spoiler" data-review-id="rw3317060" data-vote-url="/title/tt0411195/review/rw3317060/vote/interesting">\n    <div class="review-container">\n        <div class="lister-item-content">\n    <div class="ipl-ratings-bar">\n            <span class="rating-other-user-rating">\n            <svg class="ipl-icon ipl-star-icon  " xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="#000000" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24">\n                <path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/>\n                <path d="M12 17.27L18.18 21l-1.64-7.03L22 9.24l-7.19-.61L12 2 9.19 8.63 2 9.24l5.46 4.73L5.82 21z"/>\n                <path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/>\n            </svg>\n                <span>9</span><span class="point-scale">/10</span>\n            </span>\n    </div>\n<a href="/review/rw3317060/"\nclass="title" > Breakfast With Kitten.\n</a>            <div class="display-name-date">\n                    <span class="display-name-link"><a href="/user/ur60028700/"\n>anaconda-40658</a></span><span class="review-date">14 September 2015</span>\n            </div>\n                <span class="spoiler-warning">Warning: Spoilers</span>\n    <div class="ipl-expander ">\n        <div class="ipl-expander__container">\n            <div class="expander-icon-wrapper spoiler-warning__control">\n                <svg class="ipl-expander__icon expander-icon " width="12" height="8" viewBox="0 0 12 8" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                     <path d="M10.197 0L6 4.304 1.803 0 0 1.85 6 8l6-6.15" fill="#2572B3" fill-rule="evenodd"/>\n                </svg>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n            <div class="content">\n                <div class="text show-more__control">Breakfast on Pluto (2005): Dir: Neil Jordan / Cast: Cillian Murphy, Liam Neeson, Stephen Rea, Brendan Gleeson, Ruth Negga: Delirious comedy about one&#39;s state of imagination. Cillian Murphy plays an Irish transvestite raised within the Catholic Church but unsuccessful attempts to fit in result in a quest to find his mother whom he has little memory of. His quest takes him to several odd encounters with strange individuals such as a rock band and a travelling magician but all episodes pass as he focuses on his ultimate desire. Although the transvestite behaviour may put off certain viewers, the film really isn&#39;t about that. It regards his mannerisms and methods of communication but ultimately it states his desire to belong. Easily one of Neil Jordan&#39;s best films with stunning locations and photography. He is known for directing films of a controversial nature. He previously made Michael Collins and In Dreams. Fantastic performance by Murphy as Kitten whose action call unwanted attention and moral speculation. Great supporting work by Liam Neeson as the Priest whom takes him in and endures the behaviour. Stephen Rea plays a magician, and Brendan Gleeson plays another colourful character on the road. Ruth Negga plays one of the female roles who is pregnant thus realizing an illusion to Murphy. Hilarious case of one&#39;s sense of belonging with images of the bizarre. Score: 9 / 10</div>\n                <div class="actions text-muted">\n                    3 out of 4 found this helpful.\n                        <span>\n                            Was this review helpful? <a href="/registration/signin"\n> Sign in</a> to vote.\n                        </span>\n                        <br/>\n                    <a href="/review/rw3317060/"\n>Permalink</a>\n                </div>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n        <div class="clear"></div>\n    </div>\n</div>\n    </div>\n    <div class="row text-center lister-working hidden">\n    </div>\n\n        <div class="load-more-data" data-key="g4w6ddbmqyzdo6ic4oxwjnbtqlum6bz53ekdv6hialc7qv35pjt6udsyoe3f3mbkb4dt3yvdactgusdawcrawee5bs3uq" data-ajaxurl="/title/tt0411195/reviews/_ajax">\n    <div class="ipl-load-more ipl-load-more--loaded">\n        <div class="ipl-load-more__load-indicator">\n    <svg class="ipl-dot-loader" width="37px" height="7px" viewBox="0 0 37 7" version="1.1" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink">\n        <g class="ipl-dot-loader__container" fill="#000000">\n            <circle class="ipl-dot-loader__dot ipl-dot-loader__dot--one" cx="3.5" cy="3.5" r="3.5"></circle>\n            <circle class="ipl-dot-loader__dot ipl-dot-loader__dot--two" cx="18.5" cy="3.5" r="3.5"></circle>\n            <circle class="ipl-dot-loader__dot ipl-dot-loader__dot--three" cx="33.5" cy="3.5" r="3.5"></circle>\n        </g>\n    </svg>\n        </div>\n    <div class="ipl-message-box ipl-message-box--alert ipl-load-more__message-box ipl-load-more__message-box--hidden">\n            <svg class="ipl-icon ipl-alert-icon  " fill="#000000" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">\n                <path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none"/>\n                <path d="M1 21h22L12 2 1 21zm12-3h-2v-2h2v2zm0-4h-2v-4h2v4z"/>\n            </svg>\n            <span class="ipl-load-more__error-text">An error has occured.
